Activity_Recognition_Using_Accelerometer_Sensor_Data_Main¶

This file contains **KERAS** - *Higher Level API Of TensorFlow* to perform **Activity Recognition on Accelerometer Sensor Data** provided by **WISDM** and **KAGGLE-UCI**.

This file contains **KERAS** - *Higher Level API Of TensorFlow* to perform **Activity Recognition on Accelerometer Sensor Data** provided by **WISDM** and **KAGGLE-UCI**

Importing Libraries¶

This module imports all the required libraries. List of libraries and their required functions are as follows:

  • Tensorflow : Using tensorflow-gpu as a backend to enhance computation.
  • Keras : Higher level api to import all the essential models to perform activity detection.
  • Numpy : To transform csv data set into required format so can be fed into the model.
  • Model Selection : Train Test Split function provided under this library used to split data in required proportion.
In [1]:

#-----------------------------Classification- WISDM----------------------------------

wisdm = np.genfromtxt("../Datasets/HAR/wisdm_labeled.csv", delimiter=',')
print(wisdm[1])
label = wisdm[1:,-1]
print(label)
filtered_data = wisdm[1:,38:45]
print(filtered_data)
train_data,test_data,train_label,test_label = train_test_split(filtered_data,label, test_size=0.2)

print(train_data)
print(train_label)
print("\nNo. of Train Labels: ",len(train_label))

order = np.argsort(np.random.random(train_label.shape))
train_data = train_data[order]
train_label = train_label[order]
print("\nTraining set: {}".format(train_data.shape))  # 4334 examples, 13 features
print("Testing set:  {}".format(test_data.shape))     # 1084 examples, 13 features

print(train_data[0])
print(train_label[0:10])

# Test data is *not* used when calculating the mean and std
mean = train_data.mean(axis=0)
std = train_data.std(axis=0)
print(mean)
print(std)
train_data = (train_data- mean) / std
test_data = (test_data - mean) / std
print(train_data[0])

In [3]:
#Modeling 1
model = keras.Sequential([
    keras.layers.Dense(64, activation=tf.nn.relu,input_shape=(train_data.shape[1],)),
    keras.layers.Dense(64, activation=tf.nn.relu),
    keras.layers.Dense(1)
])
loss      = keras.losses.mean_absolute_error
optimizer = tf.train.RMSPropOptimizer(0.001)
metrics   = ['mae','acc']

model.compile(optimizer=optimizer,loss=loss,metrics=metrics)
model.fit(train_data, train_label, epochs=500)

model.summary()

score = model.evaluate(train_data, train_label, batch_size=128)
print("\nScore: ",score)

#Testing
test_loss,mean_error, test_acc = model.evaluate(test_data, test_label)
print('\nTest Loss:', test_loss)
print('\nTest Error:', mean_error)
print('\nTest Accuracy:', test_acc)

predictions = model.predict(test_data)
print("\nPredicted: ",predictions[500])
print("Actual Label   : ",test_label[500])

#Modeling 2
model = keras.Sequential([
    keras.layers.Dense(128, activation=tf.nn.relu),
    keras.layers.Dense(10, activation=tf.nn.softmax)])

loss      = keras.losses.sparse_categorical_crossentropy
metrics   = ['mae','acc']
optimizer = tf.train.AdamOptimizer(0.001)

model.compile(optimizer=optimizer,loss=loss,metrics=metrics)
model.fit(train_data, train_label, epochs=500)

model.summary()

score = model.evaluate(train_data, train_label, batch_size=128)
print("\nScore: ",score)

#Testing
test_loss,mean_error, test_acc = model.evaluate(test_data, test_label)
print('\nTest Loss:', test_loss)
print('\nTest Error:', mean_error)
print('\nTest Accuracy:', test_acc)

predictions = model.predict(test_data)
print("\nPredicted: ",predictions[500])
print("\nPredicted Label: ",np.argmax(predictions[500]))
print("Actual Label   : ",test_label[500])

#Modeling 3
model = keras.Sequential([
    keras.layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
    keras.layers.Dropout(0.5),
    keras.layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
    keras.layers.Dropout(0.5),
    keras.layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')])

loss      = keras.losses.sparse_categorical_crossentropy
metrics   = ['mae','acc']
optimizer = keras.optimizers.SGD(lr=0.001, decay=1e-6, momentum=0.9, nesterov=True)

model.compile(optimizer=optimizer,loss=loss,metrics=metrics)
model.fit(train_data, train_label, epochs=500)

model.summary()

score = model.evaluate(train_data, train_label, batch_size=128)
print("\nScore: ",score)

#Testing
test_loss,mean_error, test_acc = model.evaluate(test_data, test_label)
print('\nTest Loss:', test_loss)
print('\nTest Error:', mean_error)
print('\nTest Accuracy:', test_acc)

predictions = model.predict(test_data)
print("\nPredicted: ",predictions[500])
print("\nPredicted Label: ",np.argmax(predictions[500]))
print("Actual Label   : ",test_label[500])

#Modeling 1
model = keras.Sequential([
    keras.layers.Dense(64, activation=tf.nn.relu,input_shape=(train_data.shape[1],)),
    keras.layers.Dense(64, activation=tf.nn.relu),
    keras.layers.Dense(1)
])
loss      = keras.losses.mean_absolute_error
optimizer = tf.train.AdamOptimizer(0.001)
optimizer = tf.train.RMSPropOptimizer(0.001)
metrics   = ['mae','acc']

model.compile(optimizer=optimizer,loss=loss,metrics=metrics)
model.fit(train_data, train_label, epochs=500)

model.summary()

score = model.evaluate(train_data, train_label, batch_size=128)
print("\nScore: ",score)

#Testing
test_loss,mean_error, test_acc = model.evaluate(test_data, test_label)
print('\nTest Loss:', test_loss)
print('\nTest Error:', mean_error)
print('\nTest Accuracy:', test_acc)

predictions = model.predict(test_data)
print("\nPredicted: ",predictions[500])
print("Actual Label   : ",test_label[500])

#Modeling 2
model = keras.Sequential([
    keras.layers.Dense(128, activation=tf.nn.relu),
    keras.layers.Dense(10, activation=tf.nn.softmax)])

loss      = keras.losses.sparse_categorical_crossentropy
metrics   = ['mae','acc']
optimizer = tf.train.AdamOptimizer(0.001)

model.compile(optimizer=optimizer,loss=loss,metrics=metrics)
model.fit(train_data, train_label, epochs=500)

model.summary()

score = model.evaluate(train_data, train_label, batch_size=128)
print("\nScore: ",score)

#Testing
test_loss,mean_error, test_acc = model.evaluate(test_data, test_label)
print('\nTest Loss:', test_loss)
print('\nTest Error:', mean_error)
print('\nTest Accuracy:', test_acc)

predictions = model.predict(test_data)
print("\nPredicted: ",predictions[500])
print("\nPredicted Label: ",np.argmax(predictions[500]))
print("Actual Label   : ",test_label[500])

#Modeling 3
model = keras.Sequential([
    keras.layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
    keras.layers.Dropout(0.5),
    keras.layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
    keras.layers.Dropout(0.5),
    keras.layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')])

loss      = keras.losses.sparse_categorical_crossentropy
metrics   = ['mae','acc']
optimizer = keras.optimizers.SGD(lr=0.01, decay=1e-6, momentum=0.9, nesterov=True)

model.compile(optimizer=optimizer,loss=loss,metrics=metrics)
model.fit(train_data, train_label, epochs=500)

model.summary()

score = model.evaluate(train_data, train_label, batch_size=128)
print("\nScore: ",score)

#Testing
test_loss,mean_error, test_acc = model.evaluate(test_data, test_label)
print('\nTest Loss:', test_loss)
print('\nTest Error:', mean_error)
print('\nTest Accuracy:', test_acc)

predictions = model.predict(test_data)
print("\nPredicted: ",predictions[500])
print("\nPredicted Label: ",np.argmax(predictions[500]))
print("Actual Label   : ",test_label[500])
